----------------------------------------
name:Gâ€râ€aâ€câ€eâ€hâ€eâ€mâ€eâ€iâ€sâ€hâ€aâ€mâ€o
info:Guestroom - Garden-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in August 2023
info:Family
info:17 Reviews
rating:1
posted:Posted August 29, 2023
msg:"Golden outside, rotten inside" is my most honest evaluation of the hotel.
During the whole trip to Hainan, I saw the beautiful sea and stayed in many hotels. The feelings were different, but all of them had their merits and left a good impression. I wanted to praise Hainan's tourism service quality as an excellent player in China, but this hotel took a scumbag route, which deeply discredited the people of Hainan and the attitude of tourism service. Five-star listing, poor service, terrible, "Northern Myanmar" fraud-like communication, delaying customers' time, dawdling, waiting, ignoring, delaying, it seems that the hotel does not have a complete management system...
After clearly receiving my friendly communication and the poor feedback from the guest room, the hotel did not attach importance to the trust with me. During my stay, there was no care and warm condolences for us. Instead, they stared at my Ctrip evaluation rights, escalated and created contradictions, until I checked out and left, they were still entangled. This low practice is disgusting and infuriating.
In the morning of check-in, I asked through Ctrip whether the room would be upgraded. I was still on the highway. In the morning, a housekeeper, Miss Chen, called first and said that it was impossible to upgrade to the room I wanted, and I could only upgrade it to the next level. The reason was "We have to wait until the evening if we haven't sold out before we can upgrade you, but you don't have to wait that late!" In fact, we arrived at the hotel at around 5pm. They were not willing to prepare a room, but gave me a bad room with poor hygiene (as shown in the picture), poor air quality, and mold. They also turned on the air conditioner in advance to remove the odor.
On WeChat, she told me that the hotel had made the bed and made some preparations for the child. I was still immersed in the good impression of the hotel housekeeper in Sanya. I accepted their arrangement on WeChat and expressed my gratitude.
When I arrived at the hotel, the front desk had no smile and charged twice the room fee without saying anything, a total of 900 yuan. When I asked questions, there was no polite explanation, but it looked like we were going to pay so much money. I checked the order and agreed. When I entered the room, I did see the prepared disposable small pieces, disposable bathtub cover, toilet ring, a bag of sugar, small toys, and I felt very happy facing the swimming poolğŸ¥³...
The nightmare began after checking in.
First of all, the welcome fruit did not welcome us on the table. After calling the front desk, I waited in the room for 40 minutes. I wasted so much time helplessly, I was supposed to visit the duty-free city.
Second, with such a long waiting time, the child wanted to do homework first, so he asked the guest room to borrow a pen; the waiting time was 30 minutes. At this time, we didn't use the room.
The waiting time for calling the service was too long, and the room was in the front desk building and not in other locations. The distance was very close. There were very few customers that day, Qionghai, Lingshui, Wanning, and Sanya. I really don't know what mentality this hotel is run with, even the service has become a decoration... It's a rip-off! Compared with Wyndham Hotel, it was full of tourists and the response was delivered within 2 minutes.
Third, Dad took the children to swim, it was dark, and there were not many people in the swimming pool. They told us that they must have swimming caps (because each hotel has different management). We expressed our understanding and were willing to buy swimming caps on the spot. However, because the hotel had deposited hundreds of yuan from us, it asked for a sky-high price, selling swimming caps for 35 yuan each, and a family of more than 100 yuan. It was really speechless. After I contacted the housekeeper, the housekeeper said that if we didn't wear swimming caps, others would think that we were favored, and hypocritically raised the price for us by 20 yuan. Finally, we bought some takeout for 6 yuan each and went swimming. It's ridiculous. Compared with Hilton, swimming caps are 10 yuan and swimming goggles are 30 yuan. This hotel can charge exorbitant prices and do whatever it wants with a few hundred more deposits!
Fourth, after swimming, I found that the hygiene in the guest room was as shown in the picture. There were five fingerprints on the windowsill. How long has it been since it was cleaned? Looking at the gray in the corners and the moldy floor mats, wow, wow, wow, wow, wow... Are you scared? Can you swallow the candy that was given to you?
It was already night, so I contacted the housekeeper. The housekeeper asked if we wanted a waiter to clean. We considered that it was 10 o'clock in the evening, and there were various things such as swimming and bathing. It was not convenient to change rooms with children. Besides, the hotel would think that we had checked in and were not necessarily willing to change rooms.
The housekeeper replied to me Prepared a small gift for us (a few bags of sugar and a headrest (we didn't need it); also said they would send us breakfast.
Then, they told me not to give a bad review because of the assessment.
Until now, I still have sympathy, understanding of the work of young people, and the hotel has some opportunities for improvement during the travel process.
Fifth, the problem of room design, the bathroom has a threshold and a door. But the large area of â€‹â€‹the bathtub and the wash basin is not designed for drainage. Therefore, when using a disposable bathtub cover, how to prevent water from splashing on the ground, keep the outside of the bathtub dry, and the bathtub can also drain? Because there is some water on the ground, the bathroom is facing the bed, and the shoes are on the bathroom floor when you walk out, so I asked the service to get a mop Come.
The waiting time at this moment is still half an hour or more.
I notified the housekeeper again, and it was already 11:30 pm, when someone came. The waiter was very unhappy and did not serve with a smile.
When she came in, I explained to her that I was sorry that the child wet the floor in the bathtub and bothered her so late.
She said with a dark face that the child had wet the bathroom, not the bathtub. Before leaving, I thanked her, and she said unhappily that when she delivered the floor mat, she saw the child taking a bath and the water was outside the bathroom. She asked her for a quilt and something else. . . . . . This is the first time I have seen such a waiter complaining to others.
The service time is more than half an hour, and you are still serious?
Compared with all In the hotel, the waiters all smiled at the children and said it was okay, that children are all like that.
Sixth, when we went out to swim and unplugged the electricity card, we found that after turning off the air conditioner, the musty smell spread in the room, which made our throats hurt. Considering that the waiting time for service was too long, we did not ask to change rooms.
As a result, the quilt rustled and the bed was very soft, which was far less comfortable than other hotels.
After a whole night, the whole family had sore throats, backaches, and headaches.
Seventh, the breakfast was also unsatisfactory. The front desk originally sold it for 88 yuan per adult and 48 yuan for children; it cost more than 200 yuan for a family. Because they did not do a good job of hygiene, they gave it to us as a gift. As a result, the greater the expectations, the greater the disappointment. Fortunately, it was just a gift The food was not fresh, and there were not many hot dishes. We only had a bowl of noodles. The family did not find anything to eat, slept well, and were in a bad mood.
You can look at the breakfast varieties of Hilton. Children under 1.4 are free. All the hotels along our way include breakfast. Even the manager personally serves us when we bring children. This place is less than one-third...~
Eighth, in the morning, I told Ctrip and the hotel room manager about the check-in situation. The housekeeper, the housekeeper and the waiter arrived in the room. The waiter did not admit what he said. I suggested that if it was in another hotel, the waiter would greet the child with a smile. Only then did the waiter apologize.
But the housekeeper just started to make a hard start on the compensation I and Ctrip proposed.
There was no condolence or care for our sore throat. No action was taken.
When we learned that we were in a hurry, we did not solve the problem as soon as possible. Maybe we did not want to solve it at all.

Ninth: We checked out at 9:30, ensuring that the room was intact. The deposit was 900-room fee 455, and the remaining 445, but the deposit was not received until 11:00. (Compared to the Wulan Hotel, which charged a 500 yuan deposit and received a refund message within 30 seconds when I handed in the room card)
No one explained or informed me during the whole process.
Tenth, the hotel had already charged me the full room fee of 455 yuan. They knew they did not do well and admitted their mistakes on the spot, but played the pity card and said that they had applied for the highest internal negotiated price with the higher authorities.
The superficial gentleness was accompanied by a cruel heart. Then they proposed another plan,
First, they asked me to agree to cancel the order on Ctrip (actually, they induced me to lose the right to comment).
They said that only in this way could they go through a process and apply for a refund of 105 yuan, which is 350 yuan.
In this case, why didn't I directly ask for a refund of 105 yuan as compensation when I left the hotel? At the scene where I took the initiative to communicate again and again, when did the housekeeper actively deal with the problem and open the door to welcome guests?
Even if I understood it as "apology" or lack of work experience, I did not take the initiative to appease our dissatisfaction with the stay first,
and there was no guarantee of our rights.
Until the subsequent phone calls and WeChat contacts, they were asking me to agree to cancel the order, not out of respect for the passengers.
Too much, too much.
We gave the agency negotiation rights to Ctrip.
They told Ctrip unilaterally that they had solved the problem when I raised it. (I guess I will be defended by the official after I write this bad review)
Before leaving, I heard the housekeeper say that breakfast was given as a gift. At that time, I felt that I really needed to help this girl.
So why should the hotel management embarrass their employees? ! ? !

Later, I was already at the port, and received brainwashed words from Ctrip customer service to negotiate with me, "The hotel has dealt with the unsatisfactory hygiene in time, and also gave you a breakfast of more than 100 yuan. You have also stayed for one night, so the hotel cannot refund the fee. If you agree to cancel the order, the hotel can give it to you at a price of 350 yuan, which is equivalent to you only paying 238 yuan for the room."
